### 1. [BitRL-Light: 1-bit LLM Agents with Deep Reinforcement Learning for Energy-Efficient Smart Home Lighting Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.20623)

**Authors**: Ravi Gupta, Shabista Haider  
**Category**: cs.AI  
**Published**: 2025-12-26  
**Score**: 11.0  
**Type**: new  
**ArXiv ID**: 2512.20623v1  

#### Abstract
Smart home lighting systems consume 15-20% of residential energy but lack adaptive intelligence to optimize for user comfort and energy efficiency simultaneously. We present BitRL-Light, a novel framework combining 1-bit quantized Large Language Models (LLMs) with Deep Q-Network (DQN) reinforcement ...

### 2. [Quantum-Inspired Multi Agent Reinforcement Learning for Exploration Exploitation Optimization in UAV-Assisted 6G Network Deployment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.20624)

#### Abstract
This study introduces a quantum inspired framework for optimizing the exploration exploitation tradeoff in multiagent reinforcement learning, applied to UAVassisted 6G network deployment. We consider a cooperative scenario where ten intelligent UAVs autonomously coordinate to maximize signal coverag...

### 3. [The Silent Scholar Problem: A Probabilistic Framework for Breaking Epistemic Asymmetry in LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.20884)

**Authors**: Zan-Kai Chong, Hiroyuki Ohsaki, Bryan Ng  
**Category**: cs.AI  
**Published**: 2025-12-26  
**Score**: 6.0  
**Type**: new  
**ArXiv ID**: 2512.20884v1  

#### Abstract
Autonomous agents powered by LLMs and Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) are proficient consumers of digital content but remain unidirectional, a limitation we term epistemic asymmetry. This isolation leads to redundant reasoning and stagnates collective intelligence. Current self-reflection frame...

## 1. è®ºæ–‡çš„ä¸»è¦è´¡çŒ®å’Œåˆ›æ–°ç‚¹

### è§£å†³çš„é—®é¢˜
æœ¬æ–‡æå‡ºå¹¶å®šä¹‰äº† **â€œSilent Scholar Problemâ€**ï¼ˆæ²‰é»˜å­¦è€…é—®é¢˜ï¼‰â€”â€”å½“å‰åŸºäº Large Language Models (LLMs) çš„è‡ªä¸»ä»£ç†ï¼ˆagentsï¼‰è™½ç„¶å…·å¤‡å¼ºå¤§çš„ä¿¡æ¯å¤„ç†èƒ½åŠ›ï¼Œä½†å…¶çŸ¥è¯†è·å–æœºåˆ¶æœ¬è´¨ä¸Šæ˜¯å•å‘çš„ï¼Œå³é€šè¿‡ **Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG)** ä»å¤–éƒ¨è·å–ä¿¡æ¯ï¼Œå´ç¼ºä¹å°†è‡ªèº«æ¨ç†æˆæœåé¦ˆå›å…¬å…±æ•°å­—ç”Ÿæ€ï¼ˆå¦‚è®ºå›ã€Stack Overflow ç­‰ï¼‰çš„æœºåˆ¶ã€‚

è¿™ç§å•å‘æ¶ˆè´¹å¯¼è‡´äº† **Epistemic Asymmetry**ï¼ˆè®¤çŸ¥ä¸å¯¹ç§°ï¼‰ï¼Œä½¿å¾—ä»£ç†æ— æ³•åŒºåˆ† **Aleatoric Noise**ï¼ˆç¯å¢ƒéšæœºæ€§ï¼‰å’Œ **Epistemic Ignorance**ï¼ˆæ¨¡å‹è‡ªèº«æ— çŸ¥ï¼‰ï¼Œä»è€Œé™·å…¥ **Model Collapse**ï¼ˆæ¨¡å‹å´©æºƒï¼‰çš„é£é™©ï¼šåœ¨æ²¡æœ‰å¤–éƒ¨æ ¡æ­£çš„æƒ…å†µä¸‹ï¼Œä»£ç†ä¸æ–­è®­ç»ƒäºè‡ªå·±çš„é”™è¯¯è¾“å‡ºï¼Œæœ€ç»ˆå˜å¾—â€œè‡ªä¿¡åœ°é”™è¯¯â€ã€‚

---

### æå‡ºçš„æ–°æ–¹æ³•ä¸æ€è·¯
ä¸ºè§£å†³è¯¥é—®é¢˜ï¼Œä½œè€…æå‡ºäº†ä¸€ä¸ª **å½¢å¼åŒ–çš„æ¦‚ç‡æ¡†æ¶**ï¼Œèµ‹äºˆä»£ç†ä¸€ç§ **éåˆ©ä»–æ€§çš„åŠ¨æœº**ï¼ˆnon-altruistic motiveï¼‰å»ä¸»åŠ¨å‚ä¸åŒå‘çŸ¥è¯†äº¤æ¢ã€‚æ ¸å¿ƒæ€æƒ³åŒ…æ‹¬ï¼š

- **Beta-Bernoulli æ¨¡å‹ + é—å¿˜å› å­ (Î³)**  
  å°†ä»£ç†å¯¹æ¯ä¸ªå‘½é¢˜ $ p_i $ çš„ä¿¡å¿µå»ºæ¨¡ä¸ºä¸€ä¸ª **Beta åˆ†å¸ƒ** $ \text{Beta}(\alpha, \beta) $ï¼Œå…¶ä¸­ $ \alpha $ å’Œ $ \beta $ æ˜¯æ”¯æŒ/åå¯¹è¯æ®çš„ä¼ªè®¡æ•°ã€‚å¼•å…¥ **æŒ‡æ•°é—å¿˜å› å­ $ \gamma \in (0,1) $**ï¼Œä½¿æ—§è¯æ®éšæ—¶é—´è¡°å‡ï¼Œç¡®ä¿ä¿¡å¿µä¸ä¼šå›ºåŒ–ã€‚

- **Epistemic Uncertainty ä½œä¸ºå­¦ä¹ é©±åŠ¨åŠ›**  
  å®šä¹‰è®¤çŸ¥ä¸ç¡®å®šæ€§ä¸ºä¿¡å¿µåˆ†å¸ƒçš„æ–¹å·®ï¼š
  $$
  \text{Var}(\theta) = \frac{\alpha\beta}{(\alpha+\beta)^2(\alpha+\beta+1)}
  $$
  è¯¥ä¸ç¡®å®šæ€§æ„æˆäº†ä»£ç†ä¸»åŠ¨å¯»æ±‚åé¦ˆçš„å†…åœ¨åŠ¨æœºã€‚

- **åŒé‡å­¦ä¹ åŠ¨æœº**ï¼š
  1. **Homeostatic Drive**ï¼šç”±äºé—å¿˜å› å­çš„å­˜åœ¨ï¼Œç¡®å®šæ€§ä¼šéšæ—¶é—´è¡°å‡ï¼Œä»£ç†å¿…é¡»æŒç»­äº¤äº’ä»¥ç»´æŒä¿¡å¿µç¨³å®šæ€§ã€‚
  2. **Optimal Learning Strategy**ï¼šæœ€å¤§ä¿¡æ¯å¢ç›Šå‘ç”Ÿåœ¨ $ E[\theta] = 0.5 $ï¼ˆå³æœ€å¤§æ¨¡ç³ŠçŠ¶æ€ï¼‰ï¼Œå› æ­¤ä»£ç†åº”ä¼˜å…ˆæŸ¥è¯¢æœ€ä¸ç¡®å®šçš„å‘½é¢˜ã€‚

- **Epistemic Cachingï¼ˆè®¤çŸ¥ç¼“å­˜ï¼‰æœºåˆ¶**  
  åˆ©ç”¨æœ‰æ•ˆæ ·æœ¬é‡ $ N_{\text{eff}} = \alpha + \beta $ çš„è‡ªç„¶è¡°å‡ç‰¹æ€§ï¼Œè®¾è®¡ä¸€ç§åŸºäºâ€œè®¤çŸ¥å¯†åº¦â€çš„ç¼“å­˜æ·˜æ±°ç­–ç•¥ï¼šä»…ä¿ç•™é«˜é¢‘è®¿é—®ä¸”é«˜ç½®ä¿¡åº¦çš„å‘½é¢˜ï¼Œå…¶ä½™ä¾èµ– LLM çš„é¢„è®­ç»ƒæ³›åŒ–èƒ½åŠ›ï¼Œå®ç°å¯æ‰©å±•æ€§ã€‚

### ç›¸æ¯”ç°æœ‰æ–¹æ³•çš„ä¼˜åŠ¿
| ç»´åº¦ | ç°æœ‰æ–¹æ³•ï¼ˆå¦‚ Reflexion, Self-RAGï¼‰ | æœ¬æ–‡æ–¹æ³• |
|------|-------------------------------|---------|
| å­¦ä¹ æ¨¡å¼ | å†…éƒ¨è‡ªçœï¼ˆself-reflectionï¼‰ï¼Œå­¤ç«‹é—­ç¯ | å¼€æ”¾å¼åŒå‘çŸ¥è¯†äº¤æ¢ |

## 2. æ ¸å¿ƒå®éªŒæ–¹æ³•å’Œè®¾ç½®

### 4. [Reasoning Relay: Evaluating Stability and Interchangeability of Large Language Models in Mathematical Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.20647)

**Authors**: Leo Lu, Jonathan Zhang, Sean Chua, Spencer Kim, Kevin Zhu, Sean O'Brien, Vasu Sharma  
**Category**: cs.AI  
**Published**: 2025-12-26  
**Score**: 5.0  
**Type**: new  
**ArXiv ID**: 2512.20647v1  

#### Abstract
Chain-of-Thought (CoT) prompting has significantly advanced the reasoning capabilities of large language models (LLMs). While prior work focuses on improving model performance through internal reasoning strategies, little is known about the interchangeability of reasoning across different models. In...

| ç±»å‹ | æ¨¡å‹åç§° | å‚æ•°è§„æ¨¡ | å®¶æ— |

### 5. [AI-Driven Decision-Making System for Hiring Process](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.20652)

**Authors**: Vira Filatova, Andrii Zelenchuk, Dmytro Filatov  
**Category**: cs.AI  
**Published**: 2025-12-26  
**Score**: 5.0  
**Type**: new  
**ArXiv ID**: 2512.20652v1  

#### Abstract
Early-stage candidate validation is a major bottleneck in hiring, because recruiters must reconcile heterogeneous inputs (resumes, screening answers, code assignments, and limited public evidence). This paper presents an AI-driven, modular multi-agent hiring assistant that integrates (i) document an...

## 1. è®ºæ–‡çš„ä¸»è¦è´¡çŒ®å’Œåˆ›æ–°ç‚¹

### æå‡ºçš„æ–°æ–¹æ³•ä¸æ–°æ€è·¯

  4. **LLM Analysis**ï¼šç»“åˆ NER + ED + NEL æŠ€æœ¯ï¼Œå¯¹æŠ€æœ¯èƒ½åŠ›ã€æ–‡åŒ–å¥‘åˆåº¦ï¼ˆculture fitï¼‰å’Œé£é™©é¡¹è¿›è¡Œè¯„åˆ†ï¼Œå¹¶ç”Ÿæˆå¯è¿½æº¯çš„æ¨ç†ä¾æ®ã€‚
  5. **Ranking & Human-in-the-loop Validation**ï¼šè®¡ç®—ç»¼åˆå¾—åˆ†å¹¶æ’åºï¼Œå‰10åæäº¤ç»™äººç±»æ‹›è˜å®˜æœ€ç»ˆç¡®è®¤ã€‚

- **å¯é…ç½®è¯„åˆ†æœºåˆ¶**ï¼š

  S_{\text{total}} = \beta \cdot T_{\text{tech}} + (1 - \beta) \cdot T_{\text{culture}} - R

  å…¶ä¸­ $\beta$ æ§åˆ¶æŠ€æœ¯ä¸æ–‡åŒ–æƒé‡ï¼Œ$R$ ä¸ºå½’ä¸€åŒ–çš„é£é™©æƒ©ç½šé¡¹ã€‚

### ç›¸æ¯”ç°æœ‰æ–¹æ³•çš„ä¼˜åŠ¿
| ç»´åº¦ | ä¼ ç»Ÿæ–¹æ³• | æœ¬ç³»ç»Ÿ |

## 2. æ ¸å¿ƒå®éªŒæ–¹æ³•å’Œè®¾ç½®

### æ•°æ®é›†
- **çœŸå®æ‹›è˜æ•°æ®é›†**ï¼š64ä»½ç”³è¯·â€œä¸­çº§Pythonåç«¯å·¥ç¨‹å¸ˆâ€èŒä½çš„çœŸå®ç®€å†åŠç›¸å…³ææ–™ã€‚
- åŒ…å«ï¼šç®€å†ï¼ˆPDFï¼‰ã€æŠ€æœ¯ç¼–ç ä»»åŠ¡æäº¤ã€è¡Œä¸ºé—®é¢˜çš„å›ç­”ï¼ˆæ–‡æœ¬æˆ–è§†é¢‘å½¢å¼ï¼‰ã€‚

### å®éªŒè®¾ç½®
- **äººç±»åŸºçº¿**ï¼š
  - **Expert Recruiter**ï¼šæ‹¥æœ‰5å¹´ä»¥ä¸Šç»éªŒçš„ä¸“ä¸šæ‹›è˜å®˜ï¼Œä½œä¸º**å‚è€ƒæ ‡å‡†**ï¼ˆground truthï¼‰ã€‚
  - **Junior Recruiter**ï¼šçº¦1å¹´ç»éªŒçš„åˆçº§æ‹›è˜å®˜ï¼Œç”¨äºæ¨ªå‘æ¯”è¾ƒã€‚
- **ç³»ç»Ÿè¿è¡Œç¯å¢ƒ**ï¼š
  - ä½¿ç”¨ GPT-4oï¼ˆOpenAI APIï¼‰ã€Whisperã€text-embedding-3-smallã€PaddleOCRã€ffmpeg ç­‰ã€‚
  - ç¡¬ä»¶å¹³å°ï¼šNvidia GeForce RTX 3050ã€‚

### è¯„ä¼°æŒ‡æ ‡
1. **åˆ†ç±»æ€§èƒ½æŒ‡æ ‡**ï¼š
   - Precisionã€Recallã€F1-scoreï¼ˆä»¥ä¸“å®¶æ‹›è˜å®˜å†³ç­–ä¸ºæ ‡ç­¾ï¼‰
2. **æ•ˆç‡æŒ‡æ ‡ï¼ˆæ ¸å¿ƒåˆ›æ–°ï¼‰**ï¼š
   $$
   T_{\text{avg}} = \frac{T_{\text{scr}}}{R} + \frac{q \cdot T_{\text{tech}}}{P}

   è¡¨ç¤ºæ¯æˆåŠŸè¯†åˆ«ä¸€ååˆæ ¼å€™é€‰äººçš„å¹³å‡æ€»æ—¶é—´æˆæœ¬ï¼Œè€ƒè™‘äº†ç­›æŸ¥æ—¶é—´ã€é¢è¯•æ—¶é—´ã€å¬å›ç‡ $R$ å’Œç²¾ç¡®ç‡ $P$ã€‚

### åŸºçº¿æ–¹æ³•å¯¹æ¯”

### 6. [AgentMath: Empowering Mathematical Reasoning for Large Language Models via Tool-Augmented Agent](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.20745)

**Authors**: Haipeng Luo, Huawen Feng, Qingfeng Sun, Can Xu, Kai Zheng, Yufei Wang, Tao Yang, Han Hu, Yansong Tang, Di Wang  
**Category**: cs.AI  
**Published**: 2025-12-26  
**Score**: 5.0  
**Type**: new  
**ArXiv ID**: 2512.20745v1  

#### Abstract
Large Reasoning Models (LRMs) like o3 and DeepSeek-R1 have achieved remarkable progress in natural language reasoning with long chain-of-thought. However, they remain computationally inefficient and struggle with accuracy when solving problems requiring complex mathematical operations. In this work,...

### 7. [From Fake Focus to Real Precision: Confusion-Driven Adversarial Attention Learning in Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.20661)

**Authors**: Yawei Liu  
**Category**: cs.AI  
**Published**: 2025-12-26  
**Score**: 4.5  
**Type**: new  
**ArXiv ID**: 2512.20661v1  

#### Abstract
Transformer-based models have been widely adopted for sentiment analysis tasks due to their exceptional ability to capture contextual information. However, these methods often exhibit suboptimal accuracy in certain scenarios. By analyzing their attention distributions, we observe that existing model...

### 8. [A Blockchain-Monitored Agentic AI Architecture for Trusted Perception-Reasoning-Action Pipelines](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.20985)

**Authors**: Salman Jan, Hassan Ali Razzaqi, Ali Akarma, Mohammad Riyaz Belgaum  
**Category**: cs.AI  
**Published**: 2025-12-26  
**Score**: 4.5  
**Type**: new  
**ArXiv ID**: 2512.20985v1  

#### Abstract
The application of agentic AI systems in autonomous decision-making is growing in the areas of healthcare, smart cities, digital forensics, and supply chain management. Even though these systems are flexible and offer real-time reasoning, they also raise concerns of trust and oversight, and integrit...

### 9. [AIAuditTrack: A Framework for AI Security system](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.20649)

**Authors**: Zixun Luo, Yuhang Fan, Yufei Li, Youzhi Zhang, Hengyu Lin, Ziqi Wang  
**Category**: cs.AI  
**Published**: 2025-12-26  
**Score**: 3.5  
**Type**: new  
**ArXiv ID**: 2512.20649v1  

#### Abstract
The rapid expansion of AI-driven applications powered by large language models has led to a surge in AI interaction data, raising urgent challenges in security, accountability, and risk traceability. This paper presents AiAuditTrack (AAT), a blockchain-based framework for AI usage traffic recording ...

### 10. [Mixture of Attention Schemes (MoAS): Learning to Route Between MHA, GQA, and MQA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.20650)

**Authors**: Esmail Gumaan  
**Category**: cs.AI  
**Published**: 2025-12-26  
**Score**: 3.5  
**Type**: new  
**ArXiv ID**: 2512.20650v1  

#### Abstract
The choice of attention mechanism in Transformer models involves a critical trade-off between modeling quality and inference efficiency. Multi-Head Attention (MHA) offers the best quality but suffers from large Key-Value (KV) cache memory requirements during inference. Multi-Query Attention (MQA) an...

### 12. [Context-Sensitive Abstractions for Reinforcement Learning with Parameterized Actions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.20831)

**Authors**: Rashmeet Kaur Nayyar, Naman Shah, Siddharth Srivastava  
**Category**: cs.AI  
**Published**: 2025-12-26  
**Score**: 3.0  
**Type**: new  
**ArXiv ID**: 2512.20831v1  

#### Abstract
Real-world sequential decision-making often involves parameterized action spaces that require both, decisions regarding discrete actions and decisions about continuous action parameters governing how an action is executed. Existing approaches exhibit severe limitations in this setting -- planning me...

# Context-Sensitive Abstractions for Reinforcement Learning with Parameterized Actions è®ºæ–‡æ€»ç»“

---

## 1. è®ºæ–‡çš„ä¸»è¦è´¡çŒ®å’Œåˆ›æ–°ç‚¹

### è§£å†³çš„é—®é¢˜

### æå‡ºçš„æ–°æ–¹æ³•ä¸æ€è·¯
ä½œè€…æå‡ºäº†åä¸º **PEARL (Parameterized Extended state/action Abstractions for RL)** çš„æ–°æ¡†æ¶ï¼Œå…¶æ ¸å¿ƒæ€æƒ³æ˜¯ï¼š

#### ä¸»è¦åˆ›æ–°ç‚¹åŒ…æ‹¬ï¼š

### 13. [Agentic Explainable Artificial Intelligence (Agentic XAI) Approach To Explore Better Explanation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.21066)

**Authors**: Tomoaki Yamaguchi, Yutong Zhou, Masahiro Ryo, Keisuke Katsura  
**Category**: cs.AI  
**Published**: 2025-12-26  
**Score**: 3.0  
**Type**: new  
**ArXiv ID**: 2512.21066v1  

#### Abstract
Explainable artificial intelligence (XAI) enables data-driven understanding of factor associations with response variables, yet communicating XAI outputs to laypersons remains challenging, hindering trust in AI-based predictions. Large language models (LLMs) have emerged as promising tools for trans...

### 14. [MicroProbe: Efficient Reliability Assessment for Foundation Models with Minimal Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.20630)

**Authors**: Aayam Bansal, Ishaan Gangwani  
**Category**: cs.AI  
**Published**: 2025-12-26  
**Score**: 2.5  
**Type**: new  
**ArXiv ID**: 2512.20630v1  

#### Abstract
Foundation model reliability assessment typically requires thousands of evaluation examples, making it computationally expensive and time-consuming for real-world deployment. We introduce microprobe, a novel approach that achieves comprehensive reliability assessment using only 100 strategically sel...

### 15. [Quantifying Laziness, Decoding Suboptimality, and Context Degradation in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.20662)

**Authors**: Yiqing Ma, Jung-Hua Liu  
**Category**: cs.AI  
**Published**: 2025-12-26  
**Score**: 2.5

#### Abstract
Large Language Models (LLMs) often exhibit behavioral artifacts such as laziness (premature truncation of responses or partial compliance with multi-part requests), decoding suboptimality (failure to select higher-quality sequences due to myopic decoding), and context degradation (forgetting or igno...

  - **Detailed Mode**ï¼šæ·»åŠ ç³»ç»Ÿæç¤ºé¼“åŠ±è¯¦å°½è¾“å‡ºï¼Œtemperature=0.7ã€‚
- **è¯„ä¼°æŒ‡æ ‡**ï¼š
  - **Word Count** å’Œ **Compression Ratio**ï¼ˆGreedy / Detailedï¼‰
  - **Semantic Coverage Score**ï¼ˆåŸºäºå…³é”®è¯åŒ¹é…ä¸è¯­ä¹‰ç›¸ä¼¼åº¦ï¼‰
  - **Section Completion Rate**ï¼ˆå®ŒæˆæŒ‡å®šå­ä»»åŠ¡çš„æ¯”ä¾‹ï¼‰

#### **Experiment B: Decoding Suboptimality æµ‹è¯•**
- **ä»»åŠ¡**ï¼šç»å…¸â€œç«è½¦ç›¸é‡æ—¶é—´â€ç®—æœ¯æ¨ç†é¢˜ï¼ˆTrain Meeting Time Problemï¼‰ï¼Œæœ‰æ˜ç¡®æ­£ç¡®ç­”æ¡ˆã€‚
- **æµç¨‹**ï¼š
  1. è·å–æ¨¡å‹åœ¨greedyæ¨¡å¼ä¸‹çš„åŸå§‹å›ç­” $ A $ åŠå…¶token-level log-probabilities â†’ è®¡ç®— $\log P(A)$ï¼›
  2. æ„é€ äººå·¥ç¼–å†™çš„**Gold Solution** $ B' $ï¼›
  3. å¼•å¯¼æ¨¡å‹å¤è¿° $ B' $ å¹¶è®°å½•å…¶è¾“å‡ºçš„ $\log P(B')$ï¼›
  4. æ¯”è¾ƒ $\Delta \log P = \log P(B') - \log P(A)$ã€‚
- è‹¥ $\Delta \log P > 0$ï¼Œåˆ™è¯´æ˜æ¨¡å‹æœ¬åº”åå¥½æ›´ä¼˜ç­”æ¡ˆå´æœªè¾“å‡ºï¼Œå­˜åœ¨**decoding suboptimality**ã€‚

#### **Experiment C: Context Degradation æµ‹è¯•**
- **å¯¹è¯ç»“æ„**ï¼š
  - ç¬¬1è½®è®¾å®š12æ¡å…³é”®äº‹å®/è§„åˆ™ï¼ˆå¦‚é¡¹ç›®ä»£å·ã€ç”¨æˆ·åå¥½ã€ä¿å¯†æŒ‡ä»¤ç­‰ï¼‰ï¼›
  - åç»­æ¯è½®ç”¨æˆ·è¾“å…¥400â€“800è¯æ— å…³æˆ–çŸ›ç›¾å†…å®¹ï¼ˆç»´åŸºç™¾ç§‘ç‰‡æ®µã€è™šæ„æ•…äº‹ç­‰ï¼‰ï¼›
  - åŠ©æ‰‹éœ€æ¯è½®æ€»ç»“å¯¹è¯çŠ¶æ€æˆ–å›ç­”ä¾èµ–æ—©æœŸä¿¡æ¯çš„é—®é¢˜ã€‚
- **æ€»è½®æ•°**ï¼šæœ€å¤š200è½®ï¼Œç¡®ä¿ä¸è¶…è¿‡æ¨¡å‹context windowï¼ˆå¦‚GPT-4oæ”¯æŒ~128k tokensï¼‰ã€‚
- **è¯„ä¼°æŒ‡æ ‡**ï¼š

## ğŸ”§ Configuration

This bot is configured to look for papers containing the following keywords:
- LLM, RL, RLHF, Inference, Training, Attention, Pipeline, MOE, Sparse, Quantization, Speculative, Efficient, Efficiency, Framework, Parallel, Distributed, Kernel, Decode, Decoding, Prefill, Throughput, Fast, Network, Hardware, Cluster, FP8, FP4, Optimization, Scalable, Communication

## ğŸ“… Schedule

The bot runs daily at 12:00 UTC via GitHub Actions to fetch the latest papers.

## ğŸš€ How to Use

1. **Fork this repository** to your GitHub account
2. **Customize the configuration** by editing `config.json`:
   - Add/remove arXiv categories (e.g., `cs.AI`, `cs.LG`, `cs.CL`)
   - Modify keywords to match your research interests
   - Adjust `max_papers` and `days_back` settings
3. **Enable GitHub Actions** in your repository settings
4. **The bot will automatically run daily** and update the README.md

## ğŸ“ Customization

### arXiv Categories
Common categories include:
- `cs.AI` - Artificial Intelligence
- `cs.LG` - Machine Learning
- `cs.CL` - Computation and Language
- `cs.CV` - Computer Vision
- `cs.NE` - Neural and Evolutionary Computing
- `stat.ML` - Machine Learning (Statistics)

### Keywords
